2026-03-28T19:40:04.4987171Z ##[group]Run # Note: There is currently no way to distinguish between undefined variables and empty strings in GitHub Actions.
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4988618Z [36;1m# Note: There is currently no way to distinguish between undefined variables and empty strings in GitHub Actions.[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4989746Z [36;1m# This limitation affects how we handle default values and empty inputs.[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4990656Z [36;1m# For more information, see: https://github.com/actions/runner/issues/924[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4991546Z [36;1m[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4992182Z [36;1m# The following logic implements the configuration priority described in the README:[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4992941Z [36;1m#[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4993251Z [36;1m# Inputs[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4993603Z [36;1m# Environment Variables[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4994029Z [36;1m# Config File[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4994391Z [36;1m# Defaults[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4994706Z [36;1m#[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4995410Z [36;1m# As noted above defaults are awkward to handle as GitHub Actions will inject those values as the input[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4996588Z [36;1m# if the caller doesn't provide them, thus if the input matches the default we don't set it as we[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4997705Z [36;1m# can't tell the difference.  Plus if we did set it when it was the default value then it could potentially[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4998952Z [36;1m# override an external environment variable, or something in the callers configuration file, which then wouldn't[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.4999974Z [36;1m# match the configuration priority that is documented.[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5000822Z [36;1mset_env_var_if_provided() {[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5001468Z [36;1m  local var_name="$1"[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5001917Z [36;1m  local input_value="$2"[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5002373Z [36;1m  local default_value="$3"[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5002769Z [36;1m[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5003226Z [36;1m  if [ -n "$input_value" ] && [ "$input_value" != "$default_value" ]; then[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5004057Z [36;1m    # If action was provided with explicit input by the caller set that[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5004971Z [36;1m    # Use printf %q to safely escape special characters and prevent command injection[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5005844Z [36;1m    printf 'export %s=%q\n' "$var_name" "$input_value" >> trivy_envs.txt[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5006438Z [36;1m  fi[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5006726Z [36;1m}[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5006998Z [36;1m[0m
2026-03-28T19:40:04.5007473Z [36;1m# Set environment variables, handling those with default values[0m
